< review>
My family and I eat here almost every day and this place is amazing!!! The staff is very kind and they all take special care of each order, also the food is very affordable. It's perfect for any budget. My Husband and Son love the pepperoni pizza and I'm in love with the subs and salads. Make sure to order a side of Retro sauce you won't be disappointed. The Retro sauce tastes like a creamy Italian red wine vinaigrette and their ranch is so rich and creamy. I would recommend this place to anyone who loves fresh made pizza dough and made to order pizza with a wide variety of fresh toppings.< /review>

< Text>
Had company luncheon planned and thought Retro pizza would be a nice change. Called and spoke with mike and was given a 500 buck estimate for 30 pizzas and salad. Needed to feed 150 people with 2 slices and salad. After meeting with mike, long story short ended up having to take on the salad myself as now my quote would only cover the 1 topping pizzas and breadsticks. But was assured the pizzas would be cut in 10ths, to insure there was enough.also made it very clear the luncheon started @ 10am, and sharp. I needed the food by 930, 945 at the latest. Was promised they would do 2 runs and make it on time, as he knew if it was late i would look bad having people wait to eat. Needles to say day of the luncheon first half of pizza and bread came at 945am. Next batch not till 1030! Of course people were waiting in line for 30 mins on their 45 min lunch. Wow. Not only when the food arrives about 3 or 4 of the pizzas ARENT EVEN CUT and the pizzas that were are cut are cut in eigths. Like wow, the point was to not need knives, it to be finger food, AND to have enough for everyone. And nope. When Mike called me to check if the food got there, he even tried to argue with me that we agreed the pizza would be cut in eigths and didnt even know what to say about the uncut pizzas. Im not a math genius, but 8 x 30 doesnt even make 300 pieces of pizza, so how could we have agreed to that??? Told him i didnt have time to arugue with him as i was trying to cut pizza for hungry people who just lost their lunch. Was super embarrassed and thankfully all 150 people understood it was not me. To top it off mike never called me back to see how he could do better or apologize. Such a shame, cuz i will never suggest them for an event again. The food was not even good and for the price paid for a ONE TOPPING NOT EVEN GOOD PIZZA, i wish i wouldda got little ceasars. < review>
I had a new stereo receiver put into my car. It took about 4 hours total, and as far as I can tell everything works great. They are an official dealer for Alpine, which comes with some perks if you buy into that brand of stereo. These include service, and an extended warranty.

I would be lying if I said the prices here are cheap; but they are for the most part fair. I got the base level Alpine CDE-151 receiver for $150, which is exactly what Alpine sells them for online, however you can get the same model on amazon for ~$90. I ended up paying about $60 in other parts required for installation (dash kit, wire harness, and antenna adapter), and $90 for labor. There was also a $7 miscellaneous charge which I am unsure of the cause.

As far as customer service goes, 10/10. The owner, David, showed me all the different options and explained the strengths and weaknesses of each unit to help me decide what I was looking for. There was never any pressure to buy more expensive models, which I really appreciate. He and his staff are very friendly and knowledgeable.< /review>

< Text>
Happiness is knowing smart food service is in our community & being able to stock your kitchen AND deep pantry. I been shopping here for over 25 years and in the last few years the store has expanded its variety immensely! When you walk into the right is a huge walk-in refrigerator with all the produce you could ever want, salad dressing, tofu, and fresh fruit. The back of the stores entire back wall is a walk in freezer with all kinds of meat, seafood, poultry, frozen desserts & fruit. To the left is another walk in fridge with beef & dairy of all kinds, eggs, specialty cheeses & luncheon meats. As you can see in pictures everything is not sold in massive amounts-often you have a choice between Large sized & XXXL. Tami runs a tight ship & is an excellent manager. <review>Not just for restaurants, great for families too. If you do any asian cooking, you should stop by to see what staples they carry.

Some gems include: 1 gallon jugs of tamari, 6 lb jugs of Seoul Kimchi (amazing, super authentic, not vegan as it does contain fish/shrimp elements). They carry a variety of rice noodles, fish sauce, plum sauce, and curry pastes too as well as dried mushrooms (shitake, porcini),

They also stock some harder to find cuts such as  pork belly and lamb shanks.

For veggies, they always have great prices on green pepper 6 packs. They stock 3 packs of daikon radish (tends to be fresher than anything you'd find in any other store in Humboldt) as well as leeks.

They also have 5 gallon tubs of ice cream for any company events or birthday parties its a great choice.<//review><gmapID>0x54d4c4f06b155c2b:0xadb78707cf94fb5a</gmapID>< rating>
